## Name

systemd.directives — Index of configuration directives

## Unit directives

Directives for configuring units, used in unit files.

Short strings which are substituted in configuration directives.

"`%%`"  
repart.d(5), systemd-system.conf(5), systemd.automount(5), systemd.dnssd(5), systemd.mount(5), systemd.swap(5), systemd.unit(5), sysupdate.d(5), sysupdate.features(5), sysusers.d(5), tmpfiles.d(5)
